add_namespace = cuba
add_namespace = cuba_news

country_event = { #Cuba Siezes Guantanamo Bay
	id = cuba.1
	title = cuba.1.t
	desc = cuba.1.d
	picture = cuba_gitmo_seizure_pic
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CUB
		USA = {
			surrender_progress > 0.8
		}
		NOT = {
			CUB = {
				owns_state = 880
				OR = {
					is_puppet = yes
					is_subject = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = USA
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Retake what is rightfully ours!
		name = cuba.1.o1
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05
		CUB = {
			transfer_state = 880
		}
		USA = {
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = cuba.2
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Let's not be too hasty
		name = cuba.1.o2
		add_war_support = -0.15
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}
